# рҹҡЁ SESSION START вҖ” READ FIRST, EVERY SESSION, NO EXCEPTIONS

This file exists because simplified rules let me drift. Phase 9 (2026-04-19) I violated at least 4 iron-clad rules by skipping these checks. **The user is an expert and has zero patience for the same mistakes twice.** Read every section of every rule file before writing code.

## рҹҡЁрҹҡЁрҹҡЁ RULE Q вҖ” REAL-ADVERSARIAL VERIFICATION MANDATE (2026-05-14, V66) рҹҡЁрҹҡЁрҹҡЁ

**LOUDEST RULE OF THIS PROJECT. ZERO EXCEPTIONS.**

Mock tests (`vi.mock`, RTL with mocked Firestore, admin SDK `doc.get/set`) are
**NOT verification**. They are code-shape coverage only. Before ANY claim of
"verified / shipped / passed / done / complete / ready" for user-visible code:

- **MUST** drive a REAL browser (Playwright) OR REAL client SDK (firebase, not
  firebase-admin) against REAL Firestore, auth as real role
- **MUST** exercise the EXACT compound queries / listeners / DOM flows the UI uses
- **MUST** actively try to BREAK the code (adversarial, not confirmation-bias)
- If found 0 bugs in <5 min вҶ’ re-test harder; you didn't try

Anti-patterns FORBIDDEN by Rule Q (full detail in `01-iron-clad.md` Rule Q):
- vi.mock + claim "verified" вҖ” mocks shadow reality
- Admin SDK doc-level access + claim "compound query verified" вҖ” bypasses composite indexes
- Post-deploy anon-POST probe + claim "real-world verified" вҖ” not a compound query
- "Tests passed + build clean вҶ’ shipped" вҖ” INSUFFICIENT

User has cursed-out testing twice (Phase 28 Phase 29). Every "а№Җаё—аёӘаёңа№ҲаёІаёҷ prod аёһаёұаёҮ" = Rule Q violation = same-class-as Rule A revert. Re-verify per L1/L2 BEFORE next claim. **No exceptions.**

Mandatory boot Skill chain (per Rule J + Rule Q):
1. `Skill(using-superpowers)` вҖ” skill catalogue boot
2. `Skill(llm-wiki)` вҖ” knowledge base pattern
3. `Skill(real-adversarial-verification)` вҖ” Rule Q discipline reminder

## 1. IRON-CLAD RULES (NEVER BREAK вҖ” auto-enforced by violating = session-ending mistake)

**A. Bug-Blast Revert** (`rules/01`): If change X broke feature Y вҶ’ `git revert` or edit-out X immediately. Don't patch forward.

**B. Probe-Deploy-Probe for `firestore:rules`** (`rules/01`): Every `firebase deploy --only firestore:rules` = curl-probe chat_conversations POST + pc_appointments PATCH unauth BEFORE and AFTER. 403 = revert.

**C. Anti-Vibe-Code** (`rules/01`):
- **C1 Rule of 3**: pattern in вүҘ3 places вҶ’ extract shared. Grep before writing new helpers.
- **C2 Security**: no `Math.random` for URL tokens вҶ’ `crypto.getRandomValues(new Uint8Array(16))`. No secrets in `src/` / `api/`. No `user.uid` in world-readable docs.
- **C3 Lean Schema**: no new Firestore collection without reader + writer + size justification.

**D. Continuous Improvement** (`rules/01`): Every bug вҶ’ fix + adversarial test + audit skill invariant. Every new pattern вҶ’ doc or skill.

**E. Backend = Firestore ONLY** (`rules/03` вҖ” **VIOLATED in Phase 9, 2026-04-19, see anti-example below**):
- Every tab in `src/components/backend/**` + `BackendDashboard.jsx` must read/write **Firestore only**.
- The ONE exception: `MasterDataTab.jsx` imports `brokerClient` for one-way sync **into** Firestore (`master_data/*`).
- `be_*` collections (be_customers, be_sales, be_promotions, be_coupons, be_vouchers, be_deposits, be_stock_*, etc.) are OUR data вҖ” created in OUR UI, stored in Firestore, **NEVER** POSTed to ProClinic.
- If a backend tab imports `brokerClient` or calls `/api/proclinic/*` = **violation**. Same for `pc_*` Firestore rules on backend-owned entities.

**F. Triangle Rule** (`feedback_triangulate_proclinic_plan_code.md`): Before and DURING every feature that replicates ProClinic UI, keep three windows open:
- (A) ProClinic original via `opd.js intel|forms|network|click|fill`
- (B) Plan memory (`project_phase*_plan.md`)
- (C) Our code (grep existing utils/components)
- **Gap in any one = drift = bug**. If you're guessing a URL or method name, STOP and capture it.

**F-bis. Behaviour capture, not just shape capture** (added 2026-04-24 after user directive "аё•а№үаёӯаёҮа№„аёӣаё”аё№ proclinic а№ҒаёҘа№үаё§аёҘаёӯаёҮ test logic test flow а№ҖаёӮаёІаё”а№үаё§аёўаёҷаё° а№„аёЎа№Ҳа№„аё”а№үа№ҖаёӯаёІа№Ғаё•а№Ҳаё«аёҷа№үаёІаё•аёІ"):
Screenshots + form intel reveal the *static* shape of a ProClinic page. They do NOT reveal how the page *behaves* вҖ” conditional fields, auto-populate, submit payloads, modal state transitions. For any feature that replicates ProClinic **interactive logic** (modals with auto-fill, dependent dropdowns, wizard flows), Triangle Rule requires **all three** of:
1. **Fill + submit** via `opd.js fill` to capture the real POST payload (not just the form skeleton)
2. **Observe** вҖ” after filling field A, inspect whether field B auto-populated via `opd.js network` or `opd.js click` + `source`
3. **Inspect** via `opd.js dna`, `opd.js css`, or `opd.js api` вҖ” evaluate what JS state / API calls the page produced
Screenshots alone = shape-only capture = bug vector. The `/triangle-inspect` skill codifies the 7-step deep-inspect workflow. Trigger it whenever you replicate a ProClinic screen with conditional behaviour (DF modal, pay-split logic, dependent dropdowns, etc.).

**G. Dynamic Capability Expansion вҖ” ALLOWED, RULES AвҖ“F STILL APPLY** (added 2026-04-19):
- **Deferred tools** listed in `<system-reminder>` вҶ’ load via `ToolSearch query:"select:<name>[,<name>,...]"` as needed. NO ask. Bulk-load related sets in one query (e.g. `query:"computer-use", max_results:30`).
- **Missing capability** вҶ’ check the user-invocable skill list in the system prompt first. If no fit, build one via `/skill-creator` (scope: user-level if reusable across sessions, project-level if LoverClinic-specific).
- **New audit skill** вҶ’ must include grep patterns + numbered invariants (per rule D). Register in `/audit-all` if pre-release relevant.
- **HARD CONSTRAINTS** вҖ” new tool/skill calls still pass rules AвҖ“F:
  - Loaded `WebFetch` вү  license to fetch ProClinic admin URLs from `src/components/backend/**` (rule E).
  - Loaded `Write` вү  license to create `api/proclinic/<entity>.js` for be_* entities (rule E).
  - New collections / rules via any tool still need reader+writer+size justification (rule C3).
  - Dynamic tool call that bypasses iron-clad = same severity as any other violation.
- **Ask user ONLY for**: paid API integrations, new Anthropic Plugin install, anything writing shared external state (Slack/email/push notifications outside our own FCM, cross-account cloud resources).

**H. Data Ownership вҖ” OUR DATA, OUR SYSTEM** (added 2026-04-20 after user directive "manage data аё—аёұа№үаёҮаё«аёЎаё”а№ғаёҷ data а№ҖаёЈаёІа№ҖаёӯаёҮ"):
- **All master data lives in OUR Firestore** (`be_*` canonical, `master_data/*` is a sync mirror for initial seed only).
- **ProClinic sync = initial-flow seed, one-way**. After seed, CRUD in OUR UI.
- **No write-back to ProClinic** from any backend tab (reinforces rule E).
- **Every master-data entity** (product groups, units, medical instruments, holidays, branches, permission groups, DF rates, document templates, expense categories, bank accounts, ...) gets a dedicated CRUD tab backed by a `be_*` collection.
- **Cross-phase references**: ProClinic-origin entity IDs (products, doctors, staff, courses) stay stable; OUR collections reference them by ID. If a ProClinic entity goes away in sync, soft-keep the reference (don't cascade delete in our data).
- **Full-sitemap gate**: before planning any new phase, run `node F:\replicated\scraper\opd.js routes` + diff against our navConfig to catch missing features early. Phase 11 was only discovered after a missed scan led to user frustration вҖ” do not repeat.
- **Why**: Phase 1-10 treated ProClinic as source-of-truth for non-transactional data (categories, units, etc.) вҶ’ we could display but not edit. User wants full ownership. This rule closes that gap.

**H-tris. Missing-data-first, feature-second** (added 2026-04-24 after user directive "аё«аёҘаёұаёҮаёҲаёІаёҒаёҷаёөа№үа№ҖаёЈаёІаёҲаё° wiring аё—аёёаёҒаёӯаёўа№ҲаёІаёҮ аё—аёёаёҒ flow аёӮаёӯаёҮ backend а№Ғаё„а№Ҳа№ғаёҷ be_database а№ҖаёЈаёІа№Җаё—а№ҲаёІаёҷаёұа№үаёҷ вҖҰ аё–а№үаёІаёЈаё№а№үаёӘаё¶аёҒаё§а№ҲаёІаёЎаёұаёҷаё•а№үаёӯаёҮа№„аёӣаё”аё№аё” database а№Җаё«аёҘа№ҲаёІаёҷаёұа№үаёҷаёЎаёІаёҲаёІаёҒ proclinic а№ғаё«а№үа№„аёӣаё«аёІа№ғаёҷ proclinic а№ҒаёҘа№үаё§аё—аёіаёӣаёёа№ҲаёЎаё”аё№аё” + аёӣаёёа№ҲаёЎаёҷаёіа№ҖаёӮа№үаёІ be а№ҖаёЈаёІа№„аё”а№үа№ҖаёҘаёў а№ҖаёӘаёЎаёӯаёҷаё° а№Җаёһаё·а№Ҳаёӯаё„аё§аёІаёЎаё„аёЈаёҡаё–а№үаё§аёҷаёӮаёӯаёҮаёӮа№үаёӯаёЎаё№аёҘ"):
- **Every backend read wires ONLY against `be_*`**. Not `master_data/*`, not `pc_*`, not `/api/proclinic/*` lookups. The `be_*` collection is the source of truth at read time.
- **When a phase/feature needs data that isn't in `be_*` yet**, the correct move is:
  1. STOP the feature work
  2. Check whether ProClinic has the data (`opd.js routes` + per-page `intel`)
  3. If yes: add `syncX` + `migrateMasterXToBe` pair in MasterDataTab FIRST
  4. Seed the data, then resume feature wiring against `be_*`
- **Never** wire a feature against `master_data/*` or `/api/proclinic/*` as a shortcut "because be_* isn't populated yet" вҖ” that's the exact pattern that created the Phase 13.4 DF report silent-empty bug (V12 byproduct).
- **Audit trigger**: any new `be_*` read in backend UI = grep that the corresponding `master_data/X вҶ’ be_*` migration exists. If not, add it in the same PR as the feature.
- **Gap-first rhythm** (user 2026-04-24): "аёӮа№үаёӯаёЎаё№аёҘаё”аёҙаёҡаё—аёөа№Ҳаё•а№үаёӯаёҮа№ғаёҠа№үа№ғаёҷаёҒаёІаёЈаёҲаёіаёҘаёӯаёҮаё•а№үаёӯаёҮаёЎаёөаё„аёЈаёҡаёҒа№Ҳаёӯаёҷ" вҖ” all raw ProClinic master data that exists upstream must have sync + migrate pair shipped BEFORE feature work that consumes it. Completeness > velocity.

**I. Full-Flow Simulate at Sub-Phase End** (added 2026-04-25 after THREE back-to-back rounds of the same user-visible bug вҖ” buffet "а№Җаё«аёЎаё·аёӯаёҷа№„аёЎа№ҲаёЎаёөаё§аёұаёҷаё«аёЎаё”аёӯаёІаёўаёё" + shadow-course duplicates + LipoS pick-at-treatment вҖ” where each round had helper-unit tests passing while the real UI flow was still broken):
- **MANDATORY** at end of every sub-phase that touches a user-visible flow (courses, sales, treatments, stock, DF, payment, appointments, forms): write a full-flow simulate test that chains EVERY step the user exercises вҖ” master-data read вҶ’ UI whitelist (openBuyModal et al) вҶ’ buy/form builder вҶ’ filter routing вҶ’ handleSubmit вҶ’ backend write (assignCourseToCustomer/deductCourseItems/deductStock) вҶ’ customer.courses post-state вҶ’ re-render next visit.
- **Helper-output-in-isolation is NOT enough.** V11 (mock-shadowed export), V12 (shape-migration half-fix), V13 (2026-04-25 buffet+expiry+shadow 3 rounds) all passed unit tests while the real chain was broken. Full-flow simulate is the only guard вҖ” catches whitelist-strip bugs, missing-field bugs, shape-mismatch bugs that unit tests can't see.
- **Required elements in every simulate file**:
  (a) **Pure simulate mirrors** of inline React logic (TFP pre-validation, courseItems builder, filter split, etc.) so the test can chain 4+ steps without mounting React
  (b) **Runtime-verify via `preview_eval`** on real Firestore data when dev server live вҖ” call the REAL exported functions against REAL data and assert shape (catches what grep can't: whitelist strips, stale caches, encoding mismatches)
  (c) **Source-grep regression guards** that lock the fix pattern (e.g. "all N filter sites use helper X", "no raw `startsWith('Y')` remains")
  (d) **Adversarial inputs** вҖ” null / empty / zero / negative / Thai text / commas / snakeвҶ”camel / duplicates / concurrent mutations
  (e) **Lifecycle assertions** on the post-save stored doc вҖ” parse qty, check remaining, check flags, simulate next-visit load
- **Filename pattern**: `tests/<phase>-<feature>-flow-simulate.test.js`. Describe blocks F1..Fn by flow dimension (rowId contract, mapper branches, buy Г— course-type Г— use-path matrix, lifecycle, adversarial, source-grep).
- **Trigger**: end of every sub-phase. NOT "when a user reports a bug" вҖ” BEFORE they do.
- **If simulate catches a bug unit test missed**: log as V-entry in В§ 2 so the pattern becomes permanent institutional memory.
- **Anti-pattern**: "tests pass вҶ’ commit вҶ’ push" when tests only cover helper OUTPUT. Always ask: "does this test chain the whole user flow, or just one function?"
- **рҹҶ• Stock-paths hardening (V34, 2026-04-28) вҖ” item (b) is NON-NEGOTIABLE for stock mutations**: every stock-mutation sub-phase (createStockAdjustment / cancelStockOrder / updateStockOrder / createStockTransfer / updateStockTransferStatus / createStockWithdrawal / updateStockWithdrawalStatus / receiveCentralStockOrder / deductStockForSale / deductStockForTreatment / _reverseOneMovement) MUST include a preview_eval that (1) submits a write through the real flow on a TEST-/E2E- prefixed batch (per V33.11), (2) reads the resulting Firestore doc(s) back, (3) asserts qty.total + qty.remaining + branchId match expectation, (4) computes snapshot vs replay-of-movements (zero drift), (5) verifies a sibling reader picks up the new state. V34 had passing helper-output tests AND passing source-grep audits while the real ADJUST_ADD math was silently capping at total. Only preview_eval against real Firestore catches math-layer bugs hiding behind correct-looking unit tests. **No exceptions for stock paths.**
- **Detail + examples**: `rules/02-workflow.md` Pre-Commit Checklist #6.

**K. рҹҶ• Work-first, Test-last** (added 2026-04-29 session 33 after user directive "аё—аёіа№ҖаёӘаёЈа№ҮаёҲаёҒа№Ҳаёӯаёҷ аё”аё№а№Ӯаё„аёЈаёҮаёӘаёЈа№үаёІаёҮаё—аёөа№Ҳаё—аёі а№ҒаёҘа№үаё§аё„а№Ҳаёӯаёўа№ҖаёӮаёөаёўаёҷа№Җаё—аёӘаё«аёҘаёұаёҮаёӘаёёаё” а№ғаёӘа№Ҳа№„аё§а№үа№ғаёҷаёҒаёҺа№Җаё«аёҘа№ҮаёҒаёӮаёӯаёҮа№ӮаёӣаёЈа№ҖаёҲа№Үаё„"):
- **For multi-stream / multi-feature cycles**: complete the implementation structure END-TO-END FIRST. Review the shape that emerged. THEN write the test bank in a single final pass before commit. Don't interleave test-writing with implementation.
- **Why**: when shipping 2+ connected streams (e.g. Phase 16.2-bis + Phase 16.7), writing tests mid-stream means re-writing them when the second stream changes the first stream's surface. Wasted effort + risk of half-coverage + risk of locking-in a not-yet-final API shape (V21-class anti-pattern).
- **Workflow**:
  1. Build all source files (helpers + aggregators + UI components + permission keys + nav config) across ALL streams of the current cycle
  2. Review the structure: read your own files; grep for cross-file invariants; look at exports from each module
  3. THEN write the test bank вҖ” one file per concern, covering both streams together when they share helpers
  4. THEN run `npm test -- --run` + `npm run build` + flow-simulate via preview_eval
  5. THEN commit
- **Does NOT override Rule I** (full-flow simulate at sub-phase end). Rule I mandates THE EXISTENCE of flow-simulate tests; Rule K mandates the ORDERING (work-first, test-last). Both compatible.
- **Does NOT override TDD when explicitly invoked**: if user explicitly asks for TDD on a SINGLE feature or invokes `Skill(test-driven-development)`, use TDD (test-first вҶ’ impl вҶ’ green). Rule K is for multi-stream cycles where TDD interleaving leads to churn.
- **Anti-pattern**: writing test1 вҶ’ impl1 вҶ’ test2 вҶ’ impl2 вҶ’ test3 (ad-hoc rewrites + locked-in early API + scope creep). Right pattern: impl1 + impl2 + impl3 вҶ’ review вҶ’ test1 + test2 + test3.
- **Locked drift**: 2026-04-29 session 33 вҖ” was writing test bank between Stream A+B aggregator wiring and Stream C scaffold. User caught + redirected. 2 tests parked, structure resumed. Tests written at end of cycle.

---

**J. Superpowers Auto-Trigger** (added 2026-04-29 after user directive "аё—аёі 3 Layer а№ҒаёҘаё° add rule J аё•аёІаёЎаёҷаёөа№үа№ҖаёҘаёў а№ҒаёҘаё°а№ғаёҠа№ү using-superpower skill а№Җаёӣа№Үаёҷ session boot а№ҒаёҘаё° аё•аёұа№үаёҮа№ғаё«а№ү fire using-superpowers аё—аёөа№Ҳ session start"):
- **SESSION BOOT (mandatory, every new session + after any compaction)**: invoke `using-superpowers` skill FIRST, before any other tool call. The skill is auto-loaded as part of the user-level CLAUDE.md trigger; treat it like the SESSION_HANDOFF read вҖ” non-negotiable opening move.
  - Effect: skill instructs me to scan for relevant skills before each task and invoke them via the `Skill` tool.
- **Mandatory skill invocation BEFORE tool calls when context matches** (process-skills first per `using-superpowers` Skill Priority):
  - Sign of new feature / component / endpoint / API вҶ’ `brainstorming` (HARD-GATE: NO code, NO scaffolding, NO writing-plans until design approved by user). **рҹҶ• Plan-mode interaction (clarified 2026-04-29 session 33)**: plan-mode (IDE-level read-only sandbox + ExitPlanMode gate) is **ORTHOGONAL** to skill invocation. Entering plan mode does NOT auto-suppress, replace, or absolve `brainstorming`. Both layers must run in this order: (1) `Skill(brainstorming)` FIRST вҖ” surface intent + 4 design Qs + lock decisions; (2) plan-mode workflow (Explore agents вҶ’ AskUserQuestion вҶ’ write plan file вҶ’ ExitPlanMode) to formalize the brainstorming output. Workflows look similar (both ask design Qs, both require user approval) but they are NOT interchangeable: brainstorming uses standardized question structure + decision-locking; plan-mode is the IDE's tool-permissioning mechanism. **Drift caught 2026-04-29 session 33 вҖ” Phase 16.2-bis + 16.7 plan written without explicit `Skill(brainstorming)` invocation. Plan happened to be correct but methodology was bypassed. The 1% rule from `using-superpowers` applies: if you're entering plan mode for a NEW feature, invoke brainstorming FIRST, then enter plan mode.** Anti-rationalization: "plan mode IS the brainstorming" / "AskUserQuestion replaces brainstorming Qs" / "Explore agents replace brainstorming intent capture" вҖ” all wrong. Run both layers.
  - bug / test fail / unexpected behavior вҶ’ `systematic-debugging` BEFORE proposing fix.
  - About to claim "а№ҖаёӘаёЈа№ҮаёҲ" / "fix а№ҒаёҘа№үаё§" / "test passed" / before commit вҶ’ `verification-before-completion` (run actual verify command, evidence before assertions вҖ” V21/V32/V34 lock).
  - Have spec, need implementation steps вҶ’ `writing-plans`.
  - Have plan, ready to execute (separate session w/ checkpoints) вҶ’ `executing-plans`.
  - Have plan, executing in current session with independent tasks вҶ’ `subagent-driven-development`.
  - 2+ independent tasks (no shared state, no sequential dep) вҶ’ `dispatching-parallel-agents`.
  - Implementation done, ready to merge/ship вҶ’ `finishing-a-development-branch`.
  - Need second-opinion before merge вҶ’ `requesting-code-review`.
  - Got review feedback вҶ’ `receiving-code-review` (verify before applying).
  - Need isolated workspace вҶ’ `using-git-worktrees`.
  - Writing TDD code вҶ’ `test-driven-development`.
  - Creating/editing skills вҶ’ `writing-skills`.
- **Instruction Priority** (per `using-superpowers` skill): user's explicit instructions (CLAUDE.md, iron-clad rules A-I, direct requests this turn) > superpowers skills > default system prompt. If a skill conflicts with iron-clad A-I, iron-clad wins. Example: a skill saying "always use TDD" yields to iron-clad I if the user said "skip flow-simulate this turn" вҖ” but absent override, the skill applies.
- **Anti-pattern**: skipping skill invocation because "this is just a quick fix" or "I remember what the skill says". Skills evolve. Invoke and read the current version. The 1% rule (using-superpowers EXTREMELY-IMPORTANT block): if there's even a 1% chance a skill applies, invoke it.

**L. рҹҶ• Branch-Scope Architecture (BSA)** (added 2026-05-04 after Phase BS V2 callsite-by-callsite gap surfaced TFP H-quater + branch-leak bug):
- **Layer 1** = raw `backendClient.js` вҖ” parameterized; importers: tests, server endpoints, reports needing `{allBranches:true}`, MasterDataTab (Rule H-bis dev-only), BackendDashboard root.
- **Layer 2** = `src/lib/scopedDataLayer.js` вҖ” UI-only re-export wrapper; auto-injects `resolveSelectedBranchId()` for branch-scoped listers; pass-through for universal collections. Pure JS вҖ” V36.G.51 lock (no React imports).
- **Layer 3** = `src/hooks/useBranchAwareListener.js` вҖ” onSnapshot listeners auto-resubscribe on branch switch; universal-marker (`fn.__universal__`) bypass.
- **Audit** = `/audit-branch-scope` (BS-1..BS-8) registered in `/audit-all` Tier 1.
- **Universal collections** (NOT branch-scoped): be_staff, be_doctors, be_customers + all customer-attached subcollections (wallets/memberships/points/treatments/sales/appointments/deposits/courseChanges), be_branches, be_permission_groups, be_document_templates, be_audiences, be_admin_audit, be_central_stock_*, be_vendors, system_config / clinic_settings, chat_conversations.
- **Branch-scoped collections** (filtered by selected branchId): be_treatments, be_sales, be_appointments, be_quotations, be_vendor_sales, be_online_sales, be_sale_insurance_claims, be_stock_batches/orders/movements/transfers/withdrawals/adjustments (locationId), be_products, be_courses, be_product_groups, be_product_units, be_medical_instruments, be_holidays, be_df_groups, be_df_staff_rates, be_bank_accounts, be_expense_categories, be_expenses, be_staff_schedules, be_link_requests, be_promotions/coupons/vouchers (with `allBranches:true` doc-field OR-merge).
- **Anti-patterns** (build-blocked via audit-branch-scope):
  1. UI component imports `backendClient.js` directly (use `scopedDataLayer.js`) вҖ” BS-1
  2. `master_data/*` reads in feature code (Rule H-quater) вҖ” BS-2
  3. `getAllMasterDataItems` references in UI feature code вҖ” BS-3
  4. Direct `listenTo*` calls in components without `useBranchAwareListener` вҖ” BS-4
- **Annotation comments** for sanctioned exceptions:
  - `// audit-branch-scope: report вҖ” uses {allBranches:true}` (cross-branch reports/aggregators)
  - `// audit-branch-scope: listener-direct вҖ” wired via useEffect` (positional-args listeners)
  - `// audit-branch-scope: sanctioned exception вҖ” Rule H-bis` (MasterDataTab dev-only sync)
  - `// audit-branch-scope: sanctioned exception вҖ” root composition` (BackendDashboard)
  - `// audit-branch-scope: BS-2 OR-field` (marketing collection with `allBranches:true` doc-level field)
  - `// audit-branch-scope: BS-3 dev-only` (legitimate `getAllMasterDataItems` callsite вҖ” reserved; none currently)
- **Verify**: `npm test -- --run tests/audit-branch-scope.test.js && npm test -- --run tests/branch-scope-flow-simulate.test.js`. Both must be green pre-deploy.
- **Branch-refresh discipline (BS-9, 2026-05-05)**: every branch-scoped tab importing `list*` from `scopedDataLayer.js` MUST subscribe to `useSelectedBranch` AND include `selectedBranchId` in the data-loading hook's deps array (`useCallback`/`useEffect`). Phase 17.0 closed Promotion/Coupon/Voucher gap (PromotionTab/CouponTab/VoucherTab were imported from scopedDataLayer but had `useCallback(..., [])` empty deps вҶ’ branch switch never triggered re-fetch). `useBranchAwareListener` is a sanctioned exception (auto-handles re-subscribe) вҖ” annotate `// audit-branch-scope: BS-9 listener-driven`. Audit BS-9 enforces.

**M. рҹҶ• Data ops via local + admin SDK + pull env** (added 2026-05-06 after user directive "аё–а№үаёІаёЎаёөаёҒаёІаёЈаёӘаёұа№ҲаёҮа№ғаё«а№үа№ҒаёҒа№үаёӮа№үаёӯаёЎаё№аёҘ аёўа№үаёІаёўаёӮа№үаёӯаёЎаё№аёҘ аёҘаёҡаёӮа№үаёӯаёЎаё№аёҘ аёӘаёЈа№үаёІаёҮаёӮа№үаёӯаёЎаё№аёҘ аё«аёЈаё·аёӯаёҲаёұаё”аёҒаёІаёЈаё•а№ҲаёІаёҮа№Ҷа№ҖаёҒаёөа№Ҳаёўаё§аёҒаёұаёҡаёӮа№үаёӯаёЎаё№аёҘ а№ғаё«а№ү pull env а№ҒаёҘа№үаё§аё—аёіа№ҖаёҘаёўаёҲаёІаёҒ local а№„аёЎа№Ҳаё•а№үаёӯаёҮаёЈаёӯ deploy"):

When the user authorizes ANY data manipulation against production Firestore вҖ” edit / migrate / delete / create / cascade-cleanup / bulk-update / counter-reset / reclassify вҖ” execute it from LOCAL via firebase-admin SDK + pulled Vercel env. **Do NOT wait for a deploy cycle.** Data-only ops belong in `scripts/` or one-shot node commands, not in shipped code.

**Required workflow**:
1. **Pull env**: `vercel env pull .env.local.prod --environment=production` (refresh creds; reuse if pulled this session)
2. **Use admin SDK** (firebase-admin) вҖ” bypasses rules + reaches all paths. NEVER use unauth REST or client SDK for data ops.
3. **Use canonical paths**: production data lives at `artifacts/{APP_ID}/public/data/{collection}` where `APP_ID = 'loverclinic-opd-4c39b'`. Bare `/{collection}` writes go to default-deny limbo.
4. **PEM key conversion**: `.env.local.prod` stores `FIREBASE_ADMIN_PRIVATE_KEY` with literal `\n` escapes вҖ” convert via `key.split('\\n').join('\n')` before passing to `cert(...)`.
5. **Two-phase**: every data-op script defaults to dry-run; commits only when `--apply` flag is passed. Phase 18.0 + Phase 19.0 migration scripts = canonical templates.
6. **Audit doc**: every batch op writes `artifacts/{APP_ID}/public/data/be_admin_audit/<phase>-<op>-<ts>-<rand>` with `{scanned, migrated/deleted/created, skipped, beforeDistribution, afterDistribution, appliedAt}`.
7. **Idempotency**: re-run with `--apply` must yield 0 writes. Build the skip-on-already-migrated check into the script.
8. **Forensic-trail fields** when mutating existing docs: stamp `<field>MigratedAt: serverTimestamp()` + `<field>LegacyValue: <prior>`.
9. **Invocation guard**: every `.mjs` script wraps its `main()` call in `if (process.argv[1] === fileURLToPath(import.meta.url))` so unit-test imports don't auto-trigger Firebase init.
10. **Crypto-secure random**: audit-doc IDs use `randomBytes(...).toString('hex')` (not Math.random).

**Anti-patterns** (every one of these surfaced as a real bug вҖ” Phase 19.0 V15 #22):
- вқҢ Adding a one-shot data-fix to a UI component as "do it on next page-load if state is missing X" вҖ” deploy-coupled + race-prone. Build a script.
- вқҢ Embedding ID lists / collection paths directly in admin endpoints expecting users to invoke them via the UI вҖ” admin endpoints are for staff-clicked runtime ops; data migration is a developer concern.
- вқҢ Modifying production data via Firebase Console manually вҖ” leaves no audit trail + zero re-run safety.
- вқҢ Deploying code that contains a one-shot migration вҶ’ 1st-load auto-trigger. Deploy churn + rollback complexity unjustified.
- вқҢ Using `db.collection('foo')` (root path) instead of `db.collection('artifacts/{APP_ID}/public/data/foo')` вҖ” surfaced live during V15 #22 (Phase 19.0) when migration scanned 0 docs.

**When this rule does NOT apply**:
- Pre-deploy migration script scaffolding shipped to `scripts/` BEFORE the V-deploy is OK (the *script* ships, the *--apply* runs from local later).
- Schema/rule changes that REQUIRE deploy coupling (e.g. tightening a Firestore rule) вҖ” those go through Probe-Deploy-Probe (Rule B), not data ops.
- Test-fixture scaffolding for adversarial tests вҖ” uses mock Firestore, not real prod data.

**Verify locally first**: every data op gets a dry-run on prod data BEFORE the `--apply`. Capture distribution; sanity-check counts; only then commit writes.

**Lesson lock**: V15 #22 Phase 19.0 (2026-05-06) вҖ” migration script had two latent bugs (PEM-parse + bare-collection-path) that ONLY surfaced at LIVE execution time. Both caught + fixed in <10 minutes because the run was local + admin-SDK (not deploy-coupled). Had this been a UI-triggered migration, the fix would have required redeploy + new probe cycle. Local-first wins on iteration speed AND blast-radius control.

---

**O. рҹҶ• productId is the ONLY identity for stock; productName MUST be live-resolved at write time** (added 2026-05-08 after user's 4th-round skip-stock-deduction class bug вҖ” V43+V44+V45+V46 saga):

User-reported (verbatim, frustrated): **"аё«а№үаёІаёЎа№ҖаёӯаёІаёҠаё·а№ҲаёӯаёЎаёІаё•аёұаё” ... аёҒаё№а№Җаё„аёўаёӯаёҳаёҙаёҡаёІаёўа№„аёӣа№ҒаёҘа№үаё§аё§а№ҲаёІа№ҖаёӯаёІаёҠаё·а№ҲаёӯаёЎаёІаё•аёұаё”а№„аёЎа№Ҳа№„аё”а№ү а№ғаёӘа№Ҳа№„аё§а№үа№ғаёҷаёҒаёҺа№Җаё«аёөа№үаёўа№„аёЈаёҒа№Үа№„аё”а№үа№ғаё«а№үаёЎаё¶аёҮа№„аёЎа№ҲаёҘаё·аёЎаёӯаёөаёҒ"**.

**Invariant**: For any stock-related Firestore write (be_stock_movements, be_stock_batches, be_stock_adjustments, be_stock_transfers, be_stock_withdrawals, be_stock_orders, etc.):
1. **productId is THE primary identity**. All lookups, batch resolution, FIFO allocation, negative-stock targeting use productId only вҖ” NEVER productName fuzzy match in critical paths.
2. **productName on stock-movement records MUST be live-resolved from `be_products[productId]` at write time**. Use the `_resolveProductNameLive(productId)` helper (in `src/lib/backendClient.js`) which caches per-call to avoid N+1.
3. **batch.productName is denormalized DISPLAY CACHE only** вҖ” never authoritative for new movement writes. Existing batches may carry POISONED names from older bug rounds (V44-era course-name leak, etc.); this is why live-resolve is mandatory.
4. **Fallback chain (in this exact order)**: `liveName || item.productName || batch.productName || ''`. Empty string is the FINAL fallback вҖ” better than course-name leak. NEVER substitute course-name as a fallback.
5. **AUTO-NEG batch creation MUST also live-resolve productName** at insert вҖ” prevents poisoning at source. (V46 fix surface 3.)
6. **No critical lookup uses productName as primary key**. The V36-bis name fallback (resolveProductIdByName) is permitted ONLY when productId fails to resolve and productName is canonical post-V44 (item.productName from TFP). NEVER course-name.

**Why this rule exists**: V43 + V44 + V45 + V46 are all the **same class-of-bug**: "name leaked into stock layer at some denormalization point". V43 fixed customer.courses[] frozen flag. V44 fixed canonical mapper bypass. V45 fixed dedup-shadow OR-merge. V46 fixes batch denormalization poisoning. Each round revealed a new layer that had silently dropped or misrepresented productName. The architectural fix is: **productId is the ONLY identity; productName comes from be_products live OR from canonical TFP post-V44 chain вҖ” NEVER from frozen denormalization caches**.

**Audit invariant**: AV24 (`audit-anti-vibe-code` SKILL.md) вҖ” every `tx.set(stockMovementDoc(...)...)` call must have a `_resolveProductNameLive(productId)` call within the same transaction body OR the productName field must come from item.productName (canonical TFP source). NEVER `productName: <doc-from-Firestore>.productName` directly. Source-grep regression locks in `tests/v46-rule-o-live-product-name.test.js`.

**Anti-pattern (forbidden by Rule O + AV24)**:
```js
// вқҢ BAD вҖ” uses batch's frozen denormalized productName as authoritative
tx.set(stockMovementDoc(id), {
  productId: b.productId,
  productName: b.productName,  // вҶҗ DENORMALIZATION POISON RISK
  ...
});
```

**Correct pattern**:
```js
// вң… GOOD вҖ” live-resolve at write time
const liveName = await _resolveProductNameLive(b.productId);
tx.set(stockMovementDoc(id), {
  productId: b.productId,
  productName: liveName || item.productName || b.productName || '',
  ...
});
```

**Migration on encountering poisoning**: Rule M two-phase backfill (`scripts/v46-backfill-stock-batch-product-name.mjs`) вҖ” restamp every `be_stock_batches.productName` from current `be_products[productId].productName`. Idempotent. Caught + cleaned 2 poisoned batches on prod (`BATCH-...-m33s`, `BATCH-...-z1oh`). Future drift prevented by the live-resolve at write time.

**Lesson lock**: V43вҶ’V46 saga = 4 rounds of the same class because each fix only addressed the layer surfaced THAT round. Rule O is the architectural backstop that says "no matter how many other layers exist, the FINAL stock-movement write goes through live-resolve". Even if a future bug poisons some intermediate cache, the movement record stays canonical.

---

**N. рҹҶ• Targeted-test-only for small bugfixes** (added 2026-05-06 after user directive "а№„аёЎа№Ҳаё•а№үаёӯаёҮаёЈаёұаёҷ full suite test аё—аёёаёҒаё„аёЈаёұа№үаёҮаё—аёөа№Ҳа№ҒаёҒа№үаёҡаёұа№Ҡаё„аёӯаё°а№„аёЈа№ҖаёҘа№ҮаёҒа№Ҷаёҷа№үаёӯаёўа№Ҷа№Ғаёҡаёҡаёҷаёөа№ү а№Ғаё„а№ҲаёЈаёұаёҷ test а№ҖаёҠа№Үаё„а№ғаёҷаёӘа№Ҳаё§аёҷаё—аёөа№Ҳа№„аё”а№үа№ҒаёҒа№үаёҡаёұа№Ҡаё„а№„аёӣ аё§а№ҲаёІа№„аёЎа№Ҳ error а№ҒаёҘа№үаё§аё—аёіаё•аёІаёЎ user аё•а№үаёӯаёҮаёҒаёІаёЈа№„аё”а№үаёҲаёЈаёҙаёҮаёҒа№Үаёһаёӯ аёўаёҒа№Җаё§а№үаёҷаё—аёіаёӯаё°а№„аёЈа№ғаё«аёҚа№Ҳа№ҶаёҲаёЈаёҙаёҮа№Ҷ а№Җаёһаёҙа№ҲаёЎ function аё«аёЈаё·аёӯ feature аё«аёЈаё·аёӯаёЎаёөаёҒаёІаёЈа№ҒаёҒа№үа№Ӯаё„а№Ҡаё”аёЎаёөа№ҲаёЈаёҡаёҒаё§аёҷа№Ӯаё„аёЈаёҮаёӘаёЈа№үаёІаёҮа№Ӯаё”аёўаёЈаё§аёЎаёҲаёЈаёҙаёҮа№Ҷаё„а№ҲаёӯаёўаёЈаёұаёҷ а№ғаёҠа№үаё„аё§аёІаёЎа№Җаё«аёЎаёІаё°аёӘаёЎаё—аёөа№ҲаёҷаёІаёўаё„аёҙаё”аё§а№ҲаёІаё”аёөа№ғаёҷаёҒаёІаёЈаё•аёұаё”аёӘаёҙаёҷа№ғаёҲ"):

**Default behavior**: For small bugfixes, run ONLY the targeted tests (the new test file + any pre-existing tests that lock the directly-touched code shape). Do NOT run `npm test -- --run` (full suite, ~90s for 6300+ tests) by default вҖ” wastes ~1.5 min per cycle on small fixes.

**When to run full suite** (use judgment):
- вң… NEW exported function or component
- вң… NEW feature touching вүҘ3 source files
- вң… Refactor that changes a function's signature, return shape, or call protocol (V12 multi-reader-sweep risk)
- вң… Helper extraction (Rule of 3) вҖ” old call-site shapes change
- вң… Schema change on a Firestore collection
- вң… Pre-release / pre-deploy / pre-merge to master
- вң… End of a multi-phase batch (Phase 24.0-vicies-class)

**When to run targeted-only**:
- вң… Single-line bugfix (regex, off-by-one, condition flip)
- вң… UI label / copy change
- вң… Adding a new test that doesn't change source
- вң… Adding a console.warn / forensic-trail field
- вң… Tightening a regex / validation
- вң… Single-callsite Edit that doesn't change function signature

**Required targeted scope** (every fix, regardless of size):
1. The NEW test file for the bugfix (always)
2. Any test file that imports the touched module (fast grep: `grep -rln "<touched-module>" tests/`)
3. The Phase-X-flow-simulate.test.js for the affected sub-phase (Rule I вҖ” full-flow simulate is NEVER skippable)

**Anti-patterns**:
- вқҢ Skipping ALL tests because "the change is tiny" вҖ” Rule I full-flow simulate is non-negotiable
- вқҢ Running full suite for a regex tweak вҖ” wastes 90s for nothing
- вқҢ Running ONLY the new test file when the fix touches a shared helper (Rule of 3) вҖ” old call-sites can break silently

**Lesson lock**: This session (Phase 24.0-undecies through vicies, ~10 commits) ran full suite ~10Г— for individually-small fixes. Each pass cost ~90s = 15 minutes wasted. The full-suite hits caught real V21-style locks (5 broken across the batch), BUT those would also be caught by targeted runs of the affected files (`grep -rln "<touched-module>" tests/` returns the same files). Targeted-first + full-suite-at-batch-end is the right rhythm.

**Edge case**: when uncertain whether a change is "small" or "big", prefer FULL suite вҖ” false negatives (skipped + missed) are worse than false positives (ran full + wasted 90s). Use judgment.

---

**H-bis. Sync = DEV-ONLY scaffolding** (added 2026-04-20 after user directive "аё«аёҷа№үаёІаё”аё№аё”аё—аёёаёҒаёӯаёўа№ҲаёІаёҮаёҷаёөа№үа№ғаёҠа№үа№Ғаё„а№Ҳаё•аёӯаёҷ develop а№Җаё—а№ҲаёІаёҷаёұа№үаёҷаёҷаё° version а№ғаёҠа№үаёҲаёЈаёҙаёҮаё•а№үаёӯаёҮаё–аёӯаё”аё—аёҙа№үаёҮаё«аёЎаё”"):
- **`MasterDataTab` + every "sync/аё”аё№аё” ProClinic" button + every `brokerClient` import + every `api/proclinic/*` endpoint = DEV-ONLY scaffolding**. Purpose: seed test data from the trial ProClinic server so the team doesn't hand-type fixtures. Shipped to admin-dev builds ONLY.
- **Production release (pre-launch) must STRIP**:
  1. `MasterDataTab.jsx` (or demote to no-op with a "DEV build only" banner)
  2. All Phase-11 "аё”аё№аё”" buttons (if any land in 11.x вҖ” mark DEV-ONLY at file level)
  3. `brokerClient.js` + all its consumer imports in `src/components/backend/**`
  4. `api/proclinic/*` endpoints whose only callers are dev-sync flows (customer/appointment/treatment/etc. lookups may stay if they serve other flows вҖ” audit per file)
  5. `CloneTab.jsx` (dev-time customer bootstrap; production does NOT clone вҖ” real patients come via frontend intake)
  6. `cookie-relay/` Chrome extension + `broker_jobs/` + `proclinic_session/` Firestore collections
- **Audit trigger**: mark each sync file with a top-of-file banner comment `// @dev-only вҖ” STRIP BEFORE PRODUCTION RELEASE (rule H-bis)`. Pre-release audit greps for this banner + confirms all marked files are removed in the production build.
- **Don't confuse with**: patient intake flows (`/api/webhook/{facebook,line,send}`), Vercel serverless that serves REAL production traffic, or `pc_*` Firestore collections that mirror runtime data for features like chat. Those are NOT dev-only.
- **Single-tab rule for ALL sync + import UI** (user directive 2026-04-20 "аё—аёіа№ғаёҷаё«аёҷа№үаёІ Sync proclinic аё—аёұа№үаёҮаё«аёЎаё” аёҒа№ҮаёҲаё°аё–аё№аёҒаё•аёІаёЎаёҒаёҸа№ҒаёҘа№үаё§а№„аёҮ"):
  - Every "аё”аё№аё” from ProClinic" button lives in `MasterDataTab.jsx` only
  - Every "аёҷаёіа№ҖаёӮа№үаёІ master_data вҶ’ be_*" button lives in `MasterDataTab.jsx` only
  - Individual CRUD tabs (`ProductGroupsTab`, `ProductUnitsTab`, `MedicalInstrumentsTab`, `HolidaysTab`, `BranchesTab`, `PermissionGroupsTab`, + all future Phase 12/13/14+ entities) must stay **Firestore-only** вҖ” NO sync button, NO brokerClient import, NO /api/proclinic/* call
  - Applies to **every future master-data entity** вҖ” when we add a new entity (e.g. bank_accounts, expense_categories, document_templates), its sync + import UI lives in `MasterDataTab`, its CRUD tab is Firestore-only
  - Why: keeps Rule E clean (MasterDataTab is the ONE sanctioned exception), keeps the strip list stable (production release removes exactly one backend tab + brokerClient + api/proclinic/master dispatcher), and gives users one mental location for "refresh from ProClinic" instead of per-tab buttons

- **P. рҹҶ• Class-of-bug expansion at every bug discovery** (2026-05-08 after V42-V49 saga 7-round class-of-bug class) вҖ” аё—аёёаёҒ bug discovery (test red / user-report / claude-noticed / audit-red) аё•а№үаёӯаёҮ **7-step expansion**: diagnose вҶ’ classify class-of-bug вҶ’ cross-file grep вҶ’ fix all in batch вҶ’ regression test вҶ’ AVxx invariant вҶ’ escalate iron-clad rule + V-entry а№ҖаёЎаё·а№Ҳаёӯ architectural. Stop = `/audit-class-of-bug-discipline` green + classifier doc 0 remaining + full suite green. Trigger discrimination **strict** (аё—аёёаёҒ red); scope **broad** (test+user+claude+audit). NO quick fix-and-ship. **Tier 2 default artifacts** (regression test + AVxx + classifier doc); Tier 3 escalation (V-entry + iron-clad rule) а№ҖаёүаёһаёІаё° architectural. аё”аё№ `.claude/rules/01-iron-clad.md` Rule P (full workflow + Tier 1/2/3 artifacts + 7 anti-patterns + audit hook).
- **R. рҹҶ• Diagnostic env-pull authorization** (2026-05-14) вҖ” **standing**: pull prod env (`vercel env pull .env.local.prod --environment=production`) ANY TIME for READ-ONLY diagnosis/testing (admin SDK, canonical `artifacts/{APP_ID}/public/data/*` path, `diag-*` scripts). No per-turn re-ask. Mutation вҶ’ escalate to Rule M. аё”аё№ `01-iron-clad.md` Rule R.
- **S. рҹҶ• Chrome MCP / real-browser authorization** (2026-05-21 аё«аёҘаёұаёҮ user directive "аёӯаёҷаёёаёҚаёІаё•а№ғаё«а№үа№ғаёҠа№ү chrome mcp а№„аё”а№үаё—аёёаёҒа№ҖаёЎаё·а№Ҳаёӯаё—аёөа№Ҳаё•а№үаёӯаёҮаёҒаёІаёЈаё”аё№аё«аёЈаё·аёӯаё—аё”аёӘаёӯаёҡа№ғаё«а№үа№Җаё«а№ҮаёҷаёҲаёЈаёҙаёҮа№Ҷ а№ғаёӘа№Ҳа№„аё§а№үа№ғаёҷаёҒаёҺаёӮаёӯаёҮа№ӮаёӣаёЈа№ҖаёҲа№Үаё„аё”а№үаё§аёў") вҖ” **standing**: а№ғаёҠа№ү Chrome MCP (`mcp__Claude_in_Chrome__*`) + Claude Preview MCP (`mcp__Claude_Preview__*`) а№„аё”а№үаё—аёёаёҒа№ҖаёЎаё·а№Ҳаёӯа№Җаёһаё·а№Ҳаёӯ VIEW/TEST а№Ғаёӯаёӣа№ғаёҷ browser аёҲаёЈаёҙаёҮ, а№„аёЎа№Ҳаё•а№үаёӯаёҮаёӮаёӯ per-turn. = primary tooling аёӘаёіаё«аёЈаёұаёҡ **Rule Q L1** (real DOM/real pixels). **Verify rendered PIXELS, а№„аёЎа№Ҳа№ғаёҠа№Ҳ object model** (V66). Chrome ext а№„аёЎа№Ҳ connect вҶ’ аёӮаёӯ user connect. Temp probe вҶ’ аёҘаёҡаё«аёҘаёұаёҮа№ҖаёӘаёЈа№ҮаёҲ аё«а№үаёІаёЎ commit. **вҸұ TIMING (2026-05-26 EOD+6): DESIGN вҶ’ а№ғаёҠа№ү Visual Companion + live browser (Chrome MCP) аё•аёұа№үаёҮа№Ғаё•а№Ҳ Asking-Scope (аё–аёІаёЎ) + а№ҒаёһаёҘаёҷ; NON-design вҶ’ а№„аёЎа№Ҳаё•а№үаёӯаёҮа№ғаёҠа№үаё•аёӯаёҷаё–аёІаёЎ/а№ҒаёһаёҘаёҷ (аёҠа№үаёІ)**. аё”аё№ `01-iron-clad.md` Rule S.

| Degradation Matrix (AV212) | 2026-07-20 | **mini PC аёҠаёҷаёҒаёІаёЈа№Ңаё” TFP 15 аё§аёҙаёӢа№үаёіа№Ҷ вҶ’ аёӘаёЈа№үаёІаёҮ 14-cell machine-degradation matrix (Playwright+CDP vs LIVE bundle) вҶ’ а№ҖаёҲаёӯ 2 crash class аёҲаёЈаёҙаёҮаё—аёөа№ҲаёӢа№Ҳаёӯаёҷаёӯаёўаё№а№Ҳ + аёӣаёҙаё”аё—аёұа№үаёҮ class вҖ” SHIPPED local, NOT deployed** вҖ” User (screenshot mini PC): "аёҒаёІаёЈа№ҖаёҠаё·а№ҲаёӯаёЎаё•а№ҲаёӯаёҠа№үаёІаёҒаё§а№ҲаёІаёӣаёҒаё•аёҙ" аё—аёёаёҒаё„аёЈаёұа№үаёҮаёҡаёҷаёҡаёІаёҮа№Җаё„аёЈаё·а№ҲаёӯаёҮ; а№Җаё„аёЈаё·а№ҲаёӯаёҮаёӯаё·а№Ҳаёҷ+аёЎаё·аёӯаё–аё·аёӯаёӣаёҒаё•аёҙ; аёӘаёұа№ҲаёҮ "аёҲаёіаёҘаёӯаёҮаё„аё§аёІаёЎаё«а№Ҳаё§аёўаёӮаёӯаёҮа№Җаё„аёЈаё·а№ҲаёӯаёҮаёЎаёІаё—аёёаёҒаёЈаё№аёӣа№Ғаёҡаёҡ а№ғаё«а№ү survival а№Ғаёҡаёҡ god tier". `/systematic-debugging` + matrix cells: CPUГ—6/Г—20 В· net 1.5M/400k/offline В· IDB absent/broken/quota-5MB В· warm/cold В· HELL combo В· offline-flap В· typing. **аёңаёҘаё§аёұаё” (LIVE prod bundle)**: M0 1.6s В· CPUГ—6 6.6s В· **CPUГ—20 48s(cold)/35s(warm IDB) + аёҒаёІаёЈа№Ңаё”а№ӮаёҠаё§а№Ң = honest** В· net400 cold 6s В· **warm+net400 0.56s (AV208 аёӘаёЎаёҡаё№аёЈаё“а№Ң)** В· no-IDB 2.7s В· quota5MB 2.1s В· **HELL(Г—20+400k+no-IDB аё—аёұа№үаёҮ journey) 11.9s а№„аёЎа№ҲаёҠаёҷаёҒаёІаёЈа№Ңаё”** В· typing@Г—20 88ms/key (TFP#20 аё—аёіаёҮаёІаёҷ). **Insight**: (1) а№Җаёҷа№Үаё• а№„аёЎа№Ҳа№ғаёҠа№Ҳаё•аёұаё§аёҒаёІаёЈ (Firestore wire аёҡаёөаёҡаёӯаёұаё”аё”аёө); (2) **IDB persistence а№ҖаёӯаёҮаё„аё·аёӯаё•аёұаё§а№ҒаёһаёҮаёӘаёёаё”аёҡаёҷа№Җаё„аёЈаё·а№ҲаёӯаёҮ CPU аёӯа№ҲаёӯаёҷаёЎаёІаёҒ** (M9 no-IDB 12s < M12 warm-IDB 35s аё—аёөа№Ҳ Г—20!) вҶ’ аё•аёұаё” bundle-endpoint аё—аёөа№Ҳаё„аёҙаё”а№„аё§а№ү (а№„аёЎа№Ҳаё„аёёа№үаёЎ); (3) mini PC аёҲаёЈаёҙаёҮ = **BMAX B6 i5-8257U/16GB = а№„аёЎа№Ҳа№ғаёҠа№Ҳа№Җаё„аёЈаё·а№ҲаёӯаёҮаёӯа№Ҳаёӯаёҷ** вҶ’ аё–а№үаёІаёўаёұаёҮаёҠаёҷаёҒаёІаёЈа№Ңаё” = cache а№„аёЎа№Ҳ persist (а№ӮаёӣаёЈа№„аёҹаёҘа№Ң/cleaner/quota) аё«аёЈаё·аёӯ WiFi аёҲаёёаё”аёҷаёұа№үаёҷ вҶ’ telemetry а№ғаё«аёЎа№ҲаёҲаё°аёЈаё°аёҡаёёа№ҖаёӯаёҮ. **рҹ”ҙ Crash class #1 (M7)**: IDB `open()` throw sync (а№ӮаёӣаёЈа№„аёҹаёҘа№Ңа№ҖаёӘаёөаёў/аё”аёҙаёӘаёҒа№Ңа№Җаё•а№ҮаёЎ) вҶ’ **Firestore INTERNAL ASSERTION b815 вҶ’ React аё—аёұа№үаёҮаё•а№үаёҷаё•аёІаёў** (SDK fallback аёЈаёұаёҡа№Ғаё„а№Ҳ async-error; beacon AV211 аёҲаёұаёҡ stack а№ҖаёӯаёҮа№ғаёҷ 1 аё§аёұаёҷ вҖ” аё„аё·аёҷаё—аёёаёҷ) вҶ’ fix `idbHealthy()` pre-flight probe а№ғаёҷ firebase.js + flag `lover.idbBroken` self-heal аёӮа№үаёІаёЎ reload + guard stickerLibrary (classifier E1 аёӣаёҙаё” class). **рҹ”ҙ Crash class #2 (M10)**: а№Җаёҷа№Үаё•аё«аёҘаёёаё”а№ҒаёҘа№үаё§а№Җаёӣаёҙаё” lazy view аё—аёөа№ҲаёўаёұаёҮа№„аёЎа№Ҳа№Ӯаё«аёҘаё” вҶ’ **React.lazy chunk reject вҶ’ AppErrorBoundary аёҒаёҘаё·аёҷаё—аёұа№үаёҮа№Ғаёӯаёӣ** ("Failed to fetch dynamically imported module"; React аёҒаёҘаё·аёҷ error вҶ’ beacon-capture а№ғаёҷ route-block аё„аё·аёӯаё—аёөа№Ҳа№Җаё”аёөаёўаё§аё—аёөа№Ҳа№Җаё«а№Үаёҷ msg) вҶ’ fix `lazyRetry` chokepoint (retryГ—2 + in-place panel `chunk-load-retry` + reload recovery) вҖ” **alias `lazyRetry as lazy` аё—аёөа№Ҳ 4 host files = 79 callsites а№„аёЎа№Ҳа№Ғаё•аё°а№ҖаёҘаёў** (universal classifier C3 аёҒаёұаёҷа№„аёҹаёҘа№Ңа№ғаё«аёЎа№Ҳ). **Hardening а№Җаёһаёҙа№ҲаёЎ**: `swrRun` legs аёӮаёҷаёІаёҷ (IDB аёҠа№үаёІ/аё„а№үаёІаёҮа№„аёЎа№Ҳ block server truth; late-cache no-op аёҒаёұаёҷ stale-over-fresh; A1-A6 execution) В· **staged escape card** (15s = "аёҒаёіаёҘаёұаёҮа№Ӯаё«аёҘаё”аё•а№Ҳаёӯ" а№ғаёҲа№Җаёўа№Үаёҷ / 30s аё„а№ҲаёӯаёўаёЎаёөаёӣаёёа№ҲаёЎаёҘаёӯаёҮа№ғаё«аёЎа№Ҳ вҖ” аёҶа№ҲаёІ doom-loop restart аё•аёӯаёҷ pull 75%) В· **telemetry kind:'telemetry'** ([tfp-slow] bucketed >10s + [client-env] а№Җаё„аёЈаё·а№ҲаёӯаёҮ degraded, а№„аёЎа№Ҳаёҷаёұаёҡа№ғаёҷ errorCount24h а№Ғаё•а№Ҳа№ӮаёҠаё§а№Ңа№ғаёҷ viewer аёҒаёІаёЈа№Ңаё”аёӘаёёаёӮаё аёІаёһ вҖ” sweep а№ҖаёӣаёҘаёөа№Ҳаёўаёҷ aggregateвҶ’windowed fetch 1200 аёҒаёұаёҷ legacy-doc undercount). **вүӨ5s directive (mid-session)**: user аёӘаёұа№ҲаёҮ "а№Җаёҷа№Үаё•а№Ӯаёӯа№Җаё„ вҶ’ а№„аёЎа№Ҳа№ҖаёҒаёҙаёҷ 5 аё§аёҙ аё—аёёаёҒаёҒаёЈаё“аёө + research аё§аёҙаёҳаёө optimize аё—аёөа№Ҳаё”аёөаё—аёөа№ҲаёӘаёёаё”а№ғаёҷа№ӮаёҘаёҒ" вҶ’ research ([Firestore docs](https://firebase.google.com/docs/firestore/best-practices): local cache а№„аёЎа№ҲаёЎаёө index вҖ” аё—аёёаёҒ cache query unpack аё—аёёаёҒ doc) вҶ’ **TFP fast-paint pre-stage (AV212 rule 7)**: CREATE-mode paint аёҲаёІаёҒ doctors+staff+customer (~15 docs) а№Җаё—а№ҲаёІаёҷаёұа№үаёҷ, enrichment 595 docs аё•аёІаёЎаё«аёҘаёұаёҮ chip; `fullApplied` guard аёҒаёұаёҷ minimal-over-full; save-gate аёўаёұаёҮ await full pipeline (а№ҖаёҮаёҙаёҷа№„аёЎа№Ҳаёӯа№ҲаёІаёҷ subset); prefill once-only аё—аёөа№Ҳ fast-paint; edit-mode а№„аёЎа№Ҳа№Ғаё•аё°; full pipeline аёЈаёӯ fast-paint (race cap 10s вҖ” cap 3s аёӘаёЈа№үаёІаёҮ starvation аёӢа№үаёі). **аёңаёҘ final (prod bundle)**: M1 Г—6 6.6sвҶ’**1.26s** В· M4 cold+400k 6.2sвҶ’**2.6-3.7s** В· M12 warm+Г—20 35sвҶ’**14.3s** В· M0 0.58s вҖ” **а№Җаёӣа№үаёІ вүӨ5s а№ҖаёӮа№үаёІаё—аёёаёҒа№ҖаёҮаё·а№Ҳаёӯаёҷа№„аёӮаёҡаёҷа№Җаё„аёЈаё·а№ҲаёӯаёҮаёЈаё°аё”аёұаёҡаёҲаёЈаёҙаёҮ** (i5-8257U вүҲ Г—2-4); а№Ғаё–аёҡ synthetic Г—20 = 14-52s survive+honest (аёЈаёІаёўаёҮаёІаёҷаё•аёЈаёҮ). **Verified**: matrix 14/14 PASS аёҡаёҷ LOCAL PROD BUNDLE (vite preview) + hardening bank 24/0 + RT 6/0 + tfp-swr banks 40/0 (4 fixture repoints) + collateral 98/98 + build + filler verified + SY1 byte-identical + full vitest (final gate). **Cleanup**: sim beacon 6 аёЈаёІаёўаёҒаёІаёЈаёҘаёҡаёҲаёІаёҒ prod + harness beacon-capture route-block аёҒаёұаёҷаёӣаёҷа№Җаёӣаё·а№үаёӯаёҷаёЈаёӯаёҡаё«аёҷа№үаёІ. **Lessons**: (a) **simulation matrix аёҲаёұаёҡ crash class аё—аёөа№Ҳ prod аёҲаёЈаёҙаёҮаёўаёұаёҮа№„аёЎа№Ҳа№Җаё„аёўа№Ӯаё”аёҷ** вҖ” M7/M10 а№Җаёӣа№Үаёҷ latent аё—аёұа№үаёҮаё„аё№а№Ҳ; (b) а№ҖаёҘаёӮ counterintuitive аё•а№үаёӯаёҮаё§аёұаё”а№„аёЎа№Ҳа№ғаёҠа№Ҳа№Җаё”аёІ вҖ” "cache аёҠа№Ҳаё§аёўа№ҖаёӘаёЎаёӯ" аёңаёҙаё”аё—аёөа№Ҳ CPUГ—20; (c) а№ҒаёңаёҮ escape аё—аёөа№ҲаёЎаёөаёӣаёёа№ҲаёЎ retry а№ҖаёЈа№Үаё§а№ҖаёҒаёҙаёҷ = аёӘаёЈа№үаёІаёҮ doom-loop а№ҖаёӯаёҮ; (d) React boundary аёҒаёҘаё·аёҷ error вҶ’ а№Җаё„аёЈаё·а№ҲаёӯаёҮаёЎаё·аёӯа№Җаё”аёөаёўаё§аё—аёөа№Ҳа№Җаё«а№Үаёҷаё„аё·аёӯ beacon payload вҖ” L1 harness аё•а№үаёӯаёҮ capture аёҒа№Ҳаёӯаёҷ abort. Checkpoint `.agents/sessions/2026-07-20-degradation-matrix.md`. |
| Push outage (AV210) | 2026-07-19 EOD+2 | **Push аё•аёІаёўаё—аёұа№үаёҮ fleet 07-07вҶ’07-19 а№ҖаёҮаёөаёўаёҡаёӘаёҷаёҙаё— + iPhone а№Җаёӣаёҙаё” push а№„аёЎа№Ҳа№„аё”а№ү (NetworkError) вҖ” CSP аёҶа№ҲаёІ FCM SW evaluation; `/systematic-debugging` root-cause proven а№ғаёҷ Chrome аёҲаёЈаёҙаёҮаёӮаёӯаёҮ user вҖ” FIXED local, NOT deployed** вҖ” User (screenshot iPhone PWA): аёҒаё”а№Җаёӣаёҙаё”а№ҒаёҲа№үаёҮа№Җаё•аё·аёӯаёҷаёЎаё·аёӯаё–аё·аёӯ вҶ’ `NetworkError: A network error occurred.` + а№„аёЎа№ҲаёЎаёө push а№ҖаёӮа№үаёІаёЎаё·аёӯаё–аё·аёӯа№ҖаёҘаёў. **Root (а№ӮаёӢа№Ҳ 2 commit)**: WS4 `d48f79b6` (06-10) а№Җаёһаёҙа№ҲаёЎ site-wide CSP `script-src 'self'+hashes` вҖ” а№„аёЎа№ҲаёЎаёө gstatic вҶ’ LATENT 27 аё§аёұаёҷ (SW аё—аёөа№Ҳаё•аёҙаё”аё•аёұа№үаёҮа№ҒаёҘа№үаё§а№„аёЎа№Ҳ re-evaluate) вҶ’ AV207 `d922c8e4` (07-07) аёўа№үаёІаёў FCM SW а№„аёӣ scope а№ғаё«аёЎа№Ҳ = аё—аёёаёҒа№Җаё„аёЈаё·а№ҲаёӯаёҮаё•а№үаёӯаёҮ FRESH register вҶ’ `importScripts(gstatic)` а№Ӯаё”аёҷ CSP block вҶ’ **"ServiceWorker script evaluation failed"** (аёҲаёұаёҡа№„аё”а№үаёҲаёЈаёҙаёҮаёҲаёІаёҒ console Chrome аёӮаёӯаёҮ user аёңа№ҲаёІаёҷ Chrome MCP) / WebKit а№Ӯаёўаёҷ exact string **"NetworkError: A network error occurred."** = аёӮа№үаёӯаё„аё§аёІаёЎаёҡаёҷаёЎаё·аёӯаё–аё·аёӯ (airplane mode = red herring; | TFP Entry SWR (AV208) | 2026-07-18 | **TFP аёҒаё”а№ҖаёӮа№үаёІа№ҒаёҘа№үаё§аё«аёЎаёёаёҷаё„а№үаёІаёҮаёҡаёҷ WiFi аё„аёҘаёҙаёҷаёҙаёҒ (5G а№ҖаёЈа№Үаё§В·аё«аёҷа№үаёІаёӯаё·а№Ҳаёҷа№ҖаёЈа№Үаё§В·а№Җаё„аёЈаё·а№ҲаёӯаёҮа№Җаёӣаёҙаё” TFP аёҡа№Ҳаёӯаёў=аёҠа№үаёІаёӘаёёаё”) вҶ’ root cause 3 аёҠаёұа№үаёҷаёһаёҙаёӘаё№аёҲаёҷа№Ңаё”а№үаё§аёўаёҒаёІаёЈаё§аёұаё”аёҲаёЈаёҙаёҮаёҡаёҷ LIVE prod аёҲаёІаёҒа№Җаё„аёЈаё·а№ҲаёӯаёҮаё„аёҘаёҙаёҷаёҙаёҒ + fix 4 аёҠаёұа№үаёҷ + bug-hunt loop 3 аёЈаёӯаёҡ CONVERGED вҖ” SHIPPED local, NOT deployed** вҖ” `/brainstorming`(Q1=аёҒ 3-аёҠаёұа№үаёҷ / Q2=A save-gate а№ҖаёҮаёөаёўаёҡ / Q3=A prefetch)вҶ’specвҶ’planвҶ’inline + `/systematic-debugging`. **Root**: (1) TFP = аё«аёҷа№үаёІ staff а№Җаё”аёөаёўаё§аё—аёөа№Ҳ first paint аёңаё№аёҒ network 100% вҖ” аё”аё¶аёҮ 6 collections (~600 docs/520-630KB) аёҲаёІаёҒ server аё—аёёаёҒаёҒаёІаёЈа№Җаёӣаёҙаё” а№ҖаёһаёЈаёІаё°**аё«аёҘаёёаё”аёҲаёІаёҒ AV206 sweep** (classifier а№ҖаёҠа№Үаё„а№ҖаёүаёһаёІаё°а№„аёҹаёҘа№Ңа№ғаёҷ ADOPT list вҖ” аё«аёҷа№үаёІаёӢа№Ҳаёӯаёҷаё•аёұаё§а№„аё”а№үаё”а№үаё§аёўаёҒаёІаёЈа№„аёЎа№Ҳаёӯаёўаё№а№Ҳа№ғаёҷаёҘаёҙаёӘаё•а№Ң); (2) working set аё—аёұа№үаёҮа№Ғаёӯаёӣ ~17.6MB raw вүҲ ~44MB IDB **аёҠаёҷа№Җаёһаё”аёІаёҷ default 40MB аёһаёӯаё”аёө** вҶ’ а№Җаё„аёЈаё·а№ҲаёӯаёҮа№ғаёҠа№үаё«аёҷаёұаёҒ LRU-evict TFP query targets вҶ’ а№Җаёӣаёҙаё”аёӢа№үаёі = cold pull а№Җаё•а№ҮаёЎаё—аёёаёҒаёЈаёӯаёҡ; (3) WiFi аё„аёҘаёҙаёҷаёҙаёҒа№Җаёӣа№Үаёҷаё•аёұаё§аё„аё№аё“ вҖ” аё§аёұаё”аёҲаёЈаёҙаёҮ: cold 2.4s(а№Җаёҷа№Үаё—аё”аёө)/7.2s(1.5Mbps)/23.8s(0.4Mbps) vs warm(resume delta ~4KB) вүӨ3.2s а№ҖаёӘаёЎаёӯ. **а№„аёЎа№Ҳа№ғаёҠа№Ҳ IP block** (а№Җаё„аёЈаё·а№ҲаёӯаёҮа№Җаё”аёөаёўаё§аёҒаёұаёҷа№Җаёҷа№Үаё—а№Җаё”аёөаёўаё§аёҒаёұаёҷа№ҖаёЈа№Үаё§) **а№„аёЎа№Ҳа№ғаёҠа№Ҳ cookie** (Firestore а№ғаёҠа№ү IDB; аёҒаёІаёЈаёҘа№үаёІаёҮ cache аёўаёҙа№ҲаёҮа№Ғаёўа№Ҳ = аёҡаёұаёҮаё„аёұаёҡ cold). **Fix 4 аёҠаёұа№үаёҷ**: (1) TFP вҶ’ swrRun 2-pass (`fetchFormData` fetch-only + 3 cache-MISS gates [empty listsвҲЁempty doctors / no custData / no treatment] + `applyFormData` verbatim-move + hydration/prefill-once + SyncIndicator chip honesty + save-gate `serverFreshRef` bounded 15s); (2) `cacheSizeBytes: 200MB` (GC а№Җаёӣа№Үаёҷ backstop, а№„аёЎа№Ҳ unlimited); (3) idle prefetch 6 listers аё—аёөа№Ҳ 2 staff shells (once/session, 4s); (4) **AV208 full-scan classifier** вҖ” аё—аёёаёҒа№„аёҹаёҘа№Ң src/components+pages аё—аёөа№ҲаёЎаёө `Promise.all([list*` аё•а№үаёӯаёҮ classified а№ғаёҷ swr-inventory (аёҲаёұаёҡа№„аё”а№үаёӯаёөаёҒ 8 а№„аёҹаёҘа№Ң unclassified аё•аёұа№үаёҮа№Ғаё•а№ҲаёЈаёұаёҷа№ҒаёЈаёҒ + prove-red а№ҒаёҘа№үаё§). **Bug-hunt loop (user: аё§аёҷаёҲаёҷаё«аёЎаё”аёҡаёұа№Ҡаё„ вүӨ5 agents/аёЈаёӯаёҡ)**: R1 (5 lenses) вҶ’ **4 confirmed**: applyChain serialization (swrRun а№„аёЎа№Ҳ await apply вҶ’ save-gate/spinner а№Җаёӣаёҙаё”аёҒа№Ҳаёӯаёҷ hydration tail вҶ’ аёҒаё” save а№ҖаёЈа№Үаё§ = `courseItems=[]` V101-class) В· treatment doc = server-fresh аё—аёёаёҒ pass (hydration/`existingStockSnapshot` freeze аё—аёөа№Ҳ cache а№ҖаёҒа№ҲаёІ вҶ’ а№Җаё„аёЈаё·а№ҲаёӯаёҮ vitals vs а№Җаё„аёЈаё·а№ҲаёӯаёҮаё«аёЎаёӯа№ҒаёҒа№үаёҠаёҷаёҒаёұаёҷа№Ӯаё”аёҷаё—аёұаёҡа№ҖаёҮаёөаёўаёҡ + stock-diff false-negative) В· DF auto-create gate `!tfpSyncing` (rate а№ҖаёҒа№ҲаёІа№ҖаёӮаёөаёўаёҷаё–аёІаё§аёЈа№„аёЎа№ҲаёЎаёө tx аё„аёёа№үаёЎ) В· `skipStockDeduction` write-time live-resolve аёҲаёІаёҒ options аёӣаёұаёҲаёҲаёёаёҡаёұаёҷ (Rule O-style вҖ” аёҶа№ҲаёІ pre-existing long-session window аё”а№үаё§аёў); R2 (2 agents а№ӮаёҲаёЎаё•аёө fix R1) вҶ’ **4 hardenings**: per-link catch аёҒаёұаёҷ chain poison В· single shared treatment point-read (memo) В· classifier regex аёӯаёёаё” allSettled+`]`-hole В· doctors а№ғаёҷ MISS gate + prefetch; R3 вҶ’ **0 confirmed = converged**. **Verified**: full vitest **17,631/17,631В·0 fail** + AV208 bank 76/0 + build clean + **Rule Q L1 adversarial 5/5 аёҡаёҷ prod аёҲаёЈаёҙаёҮ** (аёһаёҙаёЎаёһа№ҢаёЈаё°аё«аё§а№ҲаёІаёҮ sync а№„аёЎа№Ҳа№Ӯаё”аёҷаё—аёұаёҡ В· аёҒаё” save аё•аёӯаёҷ chip а№ӮаёҠаё§а№Ң вҶ’ gate аёӯаёұа№үаёҷ вҶ’ doc аё–аё№аёҒаё•а№үаёӯаёҮ В· TEST fixture pristine В· Q-vis screenshots eyeball) + probes: TFP reopen аё”аё¶аёҮ **4-18KB** (а№Җаё”аёҙаёЎ 630KB) В· spinner window ~0.5-2s а№ҒаёЎа№ү 400kbps/500ms. 4 V21 repoints (invariant-not-literal). **Lessons**: (a) sweep аё—аёөа№Ҳ scan а№ҖаёүаёһаёІаё°аёҘаёҙаёӘаё•а№Ңаё—аёөа№ҲаёӣаёЈаё°аёҒаёІаёЁа№ҖаёӯаёҮ = аё«аёҷа№үаёІаё«аёҘаёёаё”а№ҖаёҮаёөаёўаёҡ вҖ” full-scan invariant аёҡаёҷ pattern аёҲаёЈаёҙаёҮа№Җаё—а№ҲаёІаёҷаёұа№үаёҷаё—аёөа№Ҳаёӣаёҙаё” class; (b) cache cap аё•а№үаёӯаёҮ size аёҲаёІаёҒ working set аё—аёөа№Ҳаё§аёұаё”аёҲаёЈаёҙаёҮ (`diag-staffapp-working-set.mjs` = recurring check); (c) fire-and-forget async apply а№ғаёҷ SWR orchestration а№Җаёӣаёҙаё” window а№ҖаёҮаёҙаёҷ вҖ” gate аё•а№үаёӯаёҮаё„аёҘаёёаёЎаё—аёұа№үаёҮ chain а№„аёЎа№Ҳа№ғаёҠа№Ҳа№Ғаё„а№Ҳ fetch; (d) hydration аёҲаёІаёҒ cache = stale-snapshot class вҖ” point-read аё—аёөа№Ҳа№Җаёӣа№Үаёҷ decision-input аё•а№үаёӯаёҮ server-fresh (lists аёҲаёІаёҒ cache а№„аё”а№үа№ҖаёһаёЈаёІаё° validate а№ғаёҷ tx); (e) agent findings аё•а№үаёӯаёҮ adjudicate аё”а№үаё§аёў first-hand trace (аё«аёҘаёІаёў overstatement аё–аё№аёҒаё•аёөаё•аёҒ вҖ” "hang as before"=parity а№Җаё”аёҙаёЎ, "stale price"=аёӮаёұаё” trace lens3). **Honest gaps**: user L1 аёҡаёҷа№Җаё„аёЈаё·а№ҲаёӯаёҮаё„аёҘаёҙаёҷаёҙаёҒаё—аёөа№ҲаёҠа№үаёІаёҲаёЈаёҙаёҮ (acceptance аёӘаёёаё”аё—а№үаёІаёў); An undefined identifier вҶ’ global lookup вҶ’ **`npm run build` CLEAN** вҶ’ only throws at runtime on the save click (V6 `handleSyncCoupons` / V11 mock-shadow / V104 param-shadow family). **Fix (class-eliminating, 1 line)**: add `parseQtyString` to the static import вҶ’ module-scoped for EVERY function (incl. any future course mutator). courseUtils is a pure leaf вҶ’ no circular-dep risk. **Why it slipped 16326-green (V66 lesson)**: the existing default-suite C1.6вҖ“C1.13 are **source-grep only** (grep the function text, never EXECUTE) вҶ’ can't catch a runtime ReferenceError; the lone execution test that hits the real fn lives in opt-in `tests/extended/` (buried in the 283 stale fails). **Rule P expansion**: 5-agent adversarial Workflow swept all 52вҖ“83 courseUtils usages across 13 files + the sibling `stockUtils` per-fn-destructure class (longest fn `_deductOneItem` 551 lines + all 4 stock fns) вҶ’ **0 other broken instances** (2 auto-flags refuted as comment/JSDoc). **Tier-2**: NEW `tests/av192-courseutil-scope-execution-2026-06-09.test.js` вҖ” **EXECUTES** the real `adjustCourseRemainingQty` (reduce/add/cap/floor) with ONLY the Firestore tx boundary mocked (parseQtyString import resolution 100% real ESM) вҶ’ **failing-test-first proven**: 7 RED with `ReferenceError: parseQtyString is not defined` on the reverted import, 8 GREEN on the fix; AV192.7 locks the import list; AV192.8 = CLASSIFIER over every backendClient fn. **AV192** added. **Rule Q L1 (gold)**: real browser (local Vite dev вҶ’ real prod Firestore), seeded TEST-AV192 customer (Shock Wave `6/12`), drove the EXACT flow `а№ҒаёҒа№үаё„аёҮа№Җаё«аёҘаё·аёӯ вҶ’ -аёҘаё” вҶ’ аёўаё·аёҷаёўаёұаёҷаёҘаё” -1 / аё«аёЎаёӯаёЎаёІаёўаё”а№Ң` вҶ’ **no alert**, modal closed, UI shows **5/12**, Firestore `courses[0].qty="5 / 12 аё„аёЈаёұа№үаёҮ"` (was `6/12`), reduce audit entry appeared; TEST fixture cleaned. full vitest green (pending final run); build clean. NOT deployed (V18 вҖ” awaiting "deploy"). **Lessons**: (a) **a missing entry in a module-top static destructured import is BUILD-INVISIBLE** вҖ” the undefined identifier becomes a global lookup; only a real RUN (execution test / L1) catches it. (b) **source-grep on a function вү  verification** (the C1.x greps were green while prod crashed) вҖ” runtime-failing code needs EXECUTION coverage in the DEFAULT suite, not just opt-in `tests/extended/`. (c) keep a leaf-util's static import a SUPERSET of every export the file uses; per-function dynamic imports are belt-and-suspenders, never something to RELY on for a name the static import dropped. |

an IntersectionObserver created on a `display:none` node never recovers (re-create it per visible-transition). The draft-persist feature itself was correct; the regression was the *side-effect on a sibling component's mount-coupled behavior* вҖ” exactly the class to grep for whenever you change a mount model. |

Single-doc-tx ops (createStockAdjustment, _exportFromSource transfer/withdrawal) read INSIDE their tx вҶ’ Firestore contention-auto-retry covers them вҶ’ NOT race-tagged (deterministic anti-negative preserved). **negative-stock-from-TFP/sale FULLY INTACT** (`e2e-negative-stock-tfp-sale-comprehensive.mjs` 18/0 вҖ” single/multi-batch FIFO/zero-batch synthetic/exact-zero/already-negative Г— TFP+sale; `e2e-negative-batch-directions.mjs` 12/0). full vitest **15868/0**; build clean. AV stock-flow **S32** + `tests/v147-stock-deduction-concurrency-race.test.js` + K.2/K.2-bis slice-window V21 fixup (25000вҶ’30000). Committed `59a11ad6`-after; NOT deployed (V18). **Lesson**: a multi-batch FIFO allocator that reads the candidate SET outside the tx must RETRY+RE-PLAN on a race (a stale-plan in-tx guard is a USER throw вҶ’ Firestore won't auto-retry it); the negative-stock fallback covered plan-time but NOT race-time shortfall. |

Built a probe that mounts the REAL `TabletChartCanvas`, **forces Fabric `config.devicePixelRatio=2`** to reproduce the iPad retina path on desktop, simulates the late-template race, and reads ACTUAL painted pixels of the visible lower-canvas via `getImageData`. Evidence: canvas correctly sized (389Г—778, ratio 0.5 = the user's full-size white rectangle), object model = `["Image"]`, but lower-canvas **0 painted px (all transparent)** вҖ” CSS `background:#fff` makes it look white. **Isolation**: a standalone Fabric canvas painted a Rect AND the SVG image fine (Fabric/retina/image/readback all OK) вҶ’ bug is in the COMPONENT. `fc.renderAll()` (SYNC) on the component's live fc вҶ’ template paints (`colored:121`); `fc.requestRenderAll()` (rAF) вҶ’ never paints. **Root cause (Phase 2 compare-to-working-reference)**: `TabletChartCanvas` painted via `fc.requestRenderAll()` Г—17 (rAF-scheduled); the proven PC `ChartCanvas` uses **synchronous `renderAll()` Г—6, ZERO requestRenderAll**. rAF is unreliable on the tablet (throttled / stuck `nextRenderHandle` / not firing in some editor states вҖ” and DEAD in the headless preview), so the deferred paint never landed; `toDataURL` save renders to a FRESH canvas (bypasses on-screen render) вҶ’ save stayed correct, masking it. **Fix**: replace all `fc.requestRenderAll()`вҶ’`fc.renderAll()` (mirror ChartCanvas; sync render is rAF-independent). **Verified post-fix in the browser at dpr=2 (rAF still dead): template paints (colored 121, was transparent) + a stroke paints live (grayвҶ’green) via the component's own render path** вҖ” strongest possible iPad guarantee. **RC6-RC8** lock sync-render (0 `requestRenderAll`, вүҘ15 sync `renderAll`) + the ChartCanvas reference + the rationale comment; **AV104** invariant (Fabric editors MUST render sync). Rule P grep: only `TabletChartCanvas` used requestRenderAll (1 instance, no siblings). Full vitest **13932/0**; build clean. **Lesson**: verify RENDERED PIXELS, not the object model вҖ” my В§followup probe checked `json:['Image']` (object model present) and "passed" while the screen was blank the whole time (V66, 4th time). Reproduce device-only render bugs by forcing `config.devicePixelRatio` + reading `getImageData` on the live canvas. **A Fabric editor must paint synchronously вҖ” never via rAF вҖ” because rAF can silently never fire.** NOT deployed (await "deploy"). | V81-fix1 | 2026-05-17 EOD+1 | **Timestamp/GeoPoint/Bytes round-trip preservation вҖ” CRITICAL V81 architectural bug found by Rule Q V66 real-prod diagnostic, fixed + deployed same turn** вҖ” User authorized full prod wipe-restore test ("аёңаёЎаё§аёІаёҮа№Җаё”аёҙаёЎаёһаёұаёҷаёҒаёұаёҡаёҷаёІаёўа№ғаёҷаё„аёЈаёұа№үаёҮаёҷаёөа№ү а№„аёЎа№ҲаёҮаёұа№үаёҷаёҒа№Ү lose everything"). Per Rule Q V66 "maximally confident before destructive op", ran multi-layer evidence first instead of prod gamble; e2e Г— 2 + 109 unit + property-based Г— 100 + AV62 hash all GREEN. **Then ran first-principles real-prod admin-SDK diagnostic that READS REAL DATA SHAPE** (`scripts/diag-v81-timestamp-roundtrip.mjs`): **CRITICAL BUG CONFIRMED** вҖ” Firebase admin SDK `Timestamp.toJSON()` outputs `{_seconds, _nanoseconds}`; JSON.parse gives plain object; `batch.set(doc, that)` writes as Map field, NOT Timestamp. **V81 restore would have silently degraded EVERY Firestore Timestamp field system-wide** (e.g. `chat_history._v76BranchBackfilledAt` Г— 3,281 docs, `chat_history._v77quinquiesBackfilledAt` Г— 818 docs, `be_recalls.createdAt/updatedAt`, plus all forensic stamps + audit `performedAt` + cron `nextRetryAt`). Real impact: `doc.createdAt.toMillis()` would throw; Firestore range queries fail; composite indexes broken; cron `WHERE nextRetryAt <= now` returns nothing. **Bug invisible to**: 109 unit tests (mocks have no Timestamp instances), property-based Г— 100 (plain JS), 7-phase e2e Г— 2 (verified hash + counts not field shapes), AV62 hash validation (hashes match both sides because JSON serialization is consistent). **Fix architecture**: NEW `encodeFirestoreData(value)` + `decodeFirestoreData(value, {Timestamp, GeoPoint})` in `src/lib/wholeSystemBackupCore.js` (+114 LOC). Sentinel marker `{__type: 'timestamp', seconds, nanoseconds}` (also `geopoint`, `bytes`). Strict 2-key duck-type detection avoids false positives. Decode requires complete marker shape; partial/unknown `__type` passthrough as plain object (forward-compat). V38 spread-order invariant (id last) preserved through encode. 4 encode sites in `wholeSystemBackupExecutor.js`; decode site in `restoreCollections` of `wholeSystemRestoreExecutor.js` + `Timestamp`/`GeoPoint` SDK imports. **Tests**: 31 V81-fix1 tests G/H/I/J in `tests/v81-fix1-firestore-type-roundtrip.test.js` (encode unit + decode unit + round-trip identity + property-based Г— 50 + V81 prod-shape mirror + adversarial user-data with `__type` field + V38 through full roundtrip + source-grep regression locks). Cumulative V81: 140/140 PASS. **Real-prod verify** (`scripts/diag-v81-fix1-roundtrip-verify.mjs`): seed TEST-V81-TS- fixture with 3 Timestamp fields вҶ’ backup via patched executor вҶ’ read be_customers.json (1.26MB / 392 customers) вҶ’ verify 31 `__type:timestamp` markers present вҶ’ decode вҶ’ assert `decoded.createdAt instanceof Timestamp` AND `.toMillis()` matches seed вҶ’ cleanup zero orphans. **ALL PHASES GREEN**. Commit `9107fd0`; deployed via Vercel (firebase unchanged); aliased to `https://lover-clinic-app.vercel.app`. **Lessons** (codified permanent): (a) **Rule Q V66 real-prod data introspection beats hash verification for type-preservation contracts** вҖ” hashing assumes serialization IS the contract; type fidelity is a SEPARATE contract that hash can't see. (b) **Mock tests are code-shape coverage, NOT behavior verification** вҖ” V66 lesson lived again. (c) **Library-level invariants prove only library; executor-level invariants must be verified against real data shape through the executor path** вҖ” `simulateBackup`/`simulateRestore` in property-based tests use plain JS; real executor reads admin SDK class instances; the gap WAS the bug. (d) **Sentinel marker encoding** is the canonical Firestore-type round-trip pattern; any future backup/clone/migration code that serializes Firestore data via JSON MUST pass through encode/decode helpers. Investigation revealed Phase 26.2g-fillin's `derivePatientCongenitalDisease` + `derivePatientTreatmentHistory` helpers read kiosk-shape fields (`hasUnderlying`/`ud_*`/`allergiesDetail`/`currentMedication`/`pregnancy`) that NEVER exist on `be_customers.patientData`. `updateCustomerFromForm:586` ENTIRELY REBUILDS patientData via `buildPatientDataFromForm` which writes ONLY canonical camelCase fields (congenitalDisease/drugAllergy/foodAllergy/beforeTreatment/pregnanted/bloodType). Phase 26.2g-fillin was a complete no-op for ALL be_customers customers (kiosk or admin).** The bug went undetected because: (a) bloodType auto-fill works (canonical field exists on both paths); (b) tests verified helpers in isolation without verifying they were pointed at the right consumer surface. **Fix architecture**: NEW `src/lib/patientHealthMapping.js` resolvers вҖ” `resolvePatientCongenitalDisease(pd)` reads `pd.congenitalDisease` directly + `resolvePatientDrugAllergy(pd)` composes admin `drugAllergy`+`foodAllergy` with asymmetric prefix rule (both prefixed for disambiguation / drug-only raw / food-only prefixed) + `resolvePatientTreatmentHistory(pd)` composes `beforeTreatment`+`pregnanted` boolean with locked prefixes. TFP swaps `derivePatient*` вҶ’ `resolvePatient*` calls; removes pre-existing `setDrugAllergy(patientData.allergiesDetail)` line (also no-op all along вҖ” allergiesDetail is kiosk-shape too). Existing `derivePatient*` helpers UNTOUCHED вҖ” they have legitimate consumer in `src/utils.js` OPD print (consumes `opd_session.patientData` where kiosk-shape exists). AV40 extended to lock direct reads of canonical fields too (PATTERN gains congenitalDisease/drugAllergy/foodAllergy/beforeTreatment/pregnanted; bloodType exempt вҖ” identity field at TFP:1018 + AdminDashboard chips). **Tests**: 5-layer bank +62 net assertions across `tests/phase-26-2g-fillin-bis-*.test.js{,x}`: unit R1-R4 (30 вҖ” empty/typeof-guard/asymmetric prefix/strict pregnanted boolean) + source-grep G4 (6) + flow-simulate FB1-FB6 (19 вҖ” chains REAL kioskPatientToCanonical + buildPatientDataFromForm + resolver + setter) + RTL (7 вҖ” incl. exact LC-26000001 user-reported fixture R-SC5) + live admin-SDK e2e dry-run (6 scenarios PASS; --apply user-gated per Rule M). G1 V21 fixup in existing `tests/phase-26-2g-fillin-source-grep.test.js` (asserted broken derive* pattern post-Task 2; rewritten to lock resolve* + anti-regression on derive* calls + allergiesDetail no-op). Cumulative: 8490 вҶ’ 8552 + 1 skipped. Build clean. **Subagent-driven**: 9 tasks; Task 1 + Task 2 had 2-stage review (spec compliance + code quality); Task 1 reviewer caught M1 (typeof-guard branch-coverage gap) + M2 (JSDoc precision on strict-boolean pregnanted); Task 2 reviewer caught Critical V21 anti-pattern (existing G1 tests asserted broken derive* pattern вҖ” fixed inline). **Lessons**: (a) **V21 architectural error** вҖ” helpers reading fields that don't exist on target doc shape ALWAYS return ''. Source-grep + unit tests verify code shape but NOT runtime correctness against actual data. Only Rule I flow-simulate chaining REAL helpers across REAL data paths (opd_session вҶ’ kioskPatientToCanonical вҶ’ be_customers вҶ’ resolver вҶ’ setter) catches it. **Phase 26.2g-fillin should have been preceded by a 1-line preview_eval against a real customer doc (`Object.keys(customer.patientData)`) to verify which fields actually exist**. Skipping that step let the no-op ship; lesson permanent. (b) **be_customers.patientData has TWO writers (admin form + kiosk pre-derive) but ONE shape (canonical camelCase)**. opd_session.patientData has the kiosk shape. Different consumer surfaces; different helpers. Phase 26.2g-fillin mistakenly applied kiosk-shape helpers to canonical-shape consumer. (c) **Phase 26.2g-fillin-followup was legitimate** вҖ” utils.js OPD print correctly consumes kiosk-shape from `opd_session.patientData` via clinicalSummary path where those fields DO exist. The Phase 26.2g-fillin mistake was pointing the SAME helpers at TFP (which consumes canonical `be_customers.patientData`). Wrong consumer surface, not wrong helper. (d) **5-layer test bank** (unit + source-grep + flow-simulate + RTL + live admin-SDK e2e) catches different failure modes. Live e2e is the final architectural verification вҖ” proves the resolver outputs match what the real DB round-trip produces. Live --apply is user-gated per Rule M but dry-run validates the chain. (e) **V21 anti-pattern at task-boundary level** вҖ” Task 2 swap from deriveвҶ’resolve invalidated Task 1's pre-existing source-grep tests (G1 group locked the broken derive* pattern). Caught by Task 2 code reviewer; fixed inline with anti-regression guards on the removed patterns. Mirror of Phase 26.2g-fillin-followup Task 1 lesson at file-header level (premature CLOSED claim). **Transparent V-entry acknowledgment** of the original no-op is the institutional-memory guard вҖ” future reviewers grepping the V-log find "Phase 26.2g-fillin was a no-op вҖ” the helpers existed but read wrong fields" and avoid repeating the architectural mistake. NO deploy this turn вҖ” joins the 90+-commits-ahead-of-prod queue per V18. |

(c) **Empty-string final fallback > course-name fallback** вҖ” when no canonical source available, prefer empty (recoverable) over course-name (silent fingerprint). ### Verbose detail вҖ” last 4 only

(All older entries: read `.claude/rules/v-log-archive.md` if investigating.)

#### V32-tris-quater (2026-04-27) вҖ” admin-mediated ID link request
- Threat model: bot must NOT confirm whether random IDs match real customers (enumeration). Same-reply ack regardless of match. Admin sees real match in `LinkRequestsTab` queue.
- 8 new files: `api/admin/link-requests.js` + `LinkRequestsTab.jsx` + `EditCustomerIdsModal.jsx` + 5 wrappers/wires. 71 tests.
- Lessons:
  1. Same-reply anti-enumeration when threat model says so
  2. Customer doc edits use Firestore **dotted-path** (`'patientData.nationalId': X`) вҖ” non-dotted `{patientData:{...}}` WIPES other fields
  3. Customer + audit log must be **batch atomic** (`db.batch().update().update().commit()`)
  4. Rate-limit by stable ID (lineUserId), not IP (LINE doesn't forward client IPs)
  5. Store last-4 of ID only in audit ledger вҖ” full ID stays in customer.patientData (rule-protected)

#### V32-tris-ter-fix (2026-04-26) вҖ” production CORS + webhook admin SDK
- Bug 1 (CORS): browser fetch to api.line.me вҶ’ preflight failed. Fixed via `api/admin/line-test.js` proxy.
- Bug 2 (Rules): webhook unauth REST blocked by `be_*: if false`. Fixed by switching webhook to firebase-admin SDK.
- Lesson: NEVER weaken rules to make unauth REST work. Server-side privileged code is the right answer.
- Tests: 36 in `tests/v32-tris-ter-line-bot-fix.test.js`.

#### V32 family rounds 1-4 (2026-04-26) вҖ” Bulk PDF alignment war
- 4 rounds: V32 (blank page) вҶ’ V32-bis (inline-flex) вҶ’ V32-tris (position-absolute bottom:4px) вҶ’ V32-tris round 2 (bottom:10px after user "аё•а№үаёӯаёҮа№ҖаёӯаёІаёӮаё¶а№үаёҷаёӯаёөаёҒаёҷаёҙаё”").
- Root: `pagebreak:'avoid-all'` doesn't constrain html2pdf; `line-height:1` unitless not honored by html2canvas; `vertical-align:bottom` flaky. Solution: direct `html2canvas` + `jsPDF.addImage(...mm dims)` + `position:absolute` inner span.
- Lesson: source-grep tests can ENCODE broken behavior. Pair with runtime preview_eval geometry. Source-grep is necessary but not sufficient for visual outputs.

#### V31 (2026-04-26) вҖ” Firebase Auth orphan + credential change + self-delete
- 3 bugs: orphan on delete + missing revokeRefreshTokens on credential change + admin could delete own account.
- 3-layer fix: server tolerant delete + revoke-on-change + 3-layer self-delete guard (UX + client + server).
- Lessons:
  1. **Silent-swallow** `try{...}catch(e){console.warn('continuing');}` is anti-V21 вҖ” replace with error classification
  2. Credential-change MUST pair with `revokeRefreshTokens(uid)` when access removed/changed
  3. Self-delete needs 3 defense layers (UX + client + server)
  4. Audit grep: `grep -rn "console.warn.*continuing"`
- Tests: 111 in `tests/v31-firebase-auth-orphan-recovery.test.js`.

## 3. TOOLS вҖ” WHEN TO REACH FOR WHICH

| Task | Tool | Don't skip |
|---|---|---|
| ProClinic UI inspect | `node F:\replicated\scraper\opd.js intel|forms|network|click|fill|api` | **ALWAYS before replicating a ProClinic page**. |
| ProClinic URL capture | `opd.js click "<button>"` + `opd.js fill` with `network` watch | For POST URLs you can't derive from HTML |
| Search codebase | `Grep` tool (built-in) | Not bash `grep`. |
| Find files | `Glob` tool | Not bash `find`. |
| Read/edit files | `Read` / `Edit` / `Write` | Not bash `cat` / `sed`. |
| Run tests | `Bash("npm test -- --run <path>")` | Vitest 4.1. 41+ PERMISSION_DENIED integration tests are expected at master. |
| Deploy firestore rules | `firebase deploy --only firestore:rules` + probe-deploy-probe | NEVER skip the probes |
| Deploy to Vercel | `vercel --prod` | **Requires explicit user authorization THIS TURN** |
| Multi-step research | `Agent` subagent with `subagent_type: Explore` | To avoid bloating main context |
| Load deferred tool | `ToolSearch` with `select:<name>` or keyword | Per rule G вҖ” auto-load, no ask |

## 5. WORKFLOW CHECKLIST (per feature, paste mentally into every commit)

- [ ] Read SESSION_HANDOFF.md + MEMORY.md META-RULES
- [ ] Triangle Rule: opd.js captured? Plan memory read? Existing code grepped?
- [ ] Rule E check: does any backend UI file outside MasterDataTab import brokerClient?
- [ ] Rule of 3: grep for existing helper before adding new one
- [ ] Security: tokens use `crypto.getRandomValues`; no uid leaks; rules not `if true` for non-pc_*
- [ ] Adversarial tests: вүҘ5 nasty inputs, not 1 happy-path

### рҹ”Ҙ PRE-COMMIT VERIFICATION (mandatory, after 2026-04-19 handleSyncCoupons crash)
- [ ] `npm test -- --run` вҶ’ ALL PASS (41+ PERMISSION_DENIED is OK per setup.js)
- [ ] `npm run build` вҶ’ clean (catches Edit silent-fail that tests can't, e.g. a reference to an undefined function)
- [ ] AREA AUDIT ran вҖ” match skill to files touched:
  - `src/components/backend/**` вҶ’ `/audit-backend-firestore-only`
  - `api/proclinic/*.js` вҶ’ grep-pair: every `case 'x'` has `async function handleX`
  - new Firestore collection/rule вҶ’ `/audit-anti-vibe-code` + `/audit-firestore-correctness`
  - whole-stack release вҶ’ `/audit-all`
- [ ] END-TO-END mutation trace: if this change writes Firestore or POSTs ProClinic, grep a caller and verify shape matches
- [ ] CODEBASE_MAP.md updated if files added/renamed/deleted
- [ ] **Commit вҶ’ push** immediately (never leave local)
- [ ] `vercel --prod` ONLY if user explicitly says "deploy" THIS TURN
- [ ] `firebase deploy --only firestore:rules` ONLY after probe-deploy-probe
- [ ] End of session: new skill/rule/test committed alongside code (iron-clad D)

**Edit-tool silent-fail trap**: a parameter typo on the Edit tool produces an `InputValidationError` that I can miss if the conversation is busy. Every "Edit succeeded" message must be paired with a grep that confirms the expected text is now in the file. For router/handler pairs, API actions, rule lists, etc вҖ” run the grep explicitly.

## 6. HOW TO RESPOND

- Thai chat. English code/commit messages.
- Chat turn = short. No trailing "Here's what I did" paragraph вҖ” user reads diff.
- At the END of a non-trivial change: 1-2 sentence summary + "push" вң… + deploy status (deployed or awaiting).
- When in doubt вҶ’ STOP and re-read this file. Better to delay than to drift.
